Motivation: 现有文本角色扮演模型虽能模仿角色风格，但无法捕捉场景氛围和渐进的紧张感，这在VR游戏和交互叙事等沉浸式应用中至关重要。

Method: 提出EBM-RL（眼-脑-口强化学习），一种基于解耦GRPO的框架，将对话过程显式分离为观察([perception])、推理([think])和话语([answer])三个阶段，并集成四种互补奖励：CLIP场景-文本对齐奖励、感知-认知奖励、答案准确率奖励和格式奖励。

Result: EBM-RL在沉浸式角色扮演基准上显著优于纯文本基线和大规模视觉语言模型，同时在视觉氛围一致性和角色真实性上均有提升；无需微调即可在领域外VideoQA基准上展现强零样本泛化能力。

Conclusion: 解耦感知-推理-表达的框架能有效增强角色扮演模型的场景感知能力，且具有良好的泛化性；同时开源了视频角色扮演对话数据集。

Abstract: Text-based role-playing models can imitate character styles, yet they often fail to reflect a scene's atmosphere and evolving tension, both essential for immersive applications such as Virtual Reality (VR) games and interactive narratives. We study video-grounded role-playing dialogue and introduce EBM-RL (Eye-Brain-Mouth Reinforcement Learning), a decoupled GRPO-based framework that explicitly separates observation ([perception]), reasoning ([think]), and utterance ([answer]). This structure promotes human-like sensory grounding by compelling the model to first attend to visual cues, then form internal interpretations, and finally generate context-appropriate dialogue.
  EBM-RL integrates four complementary rewards: (i) CLIP-based scene-text alignment to improve ambiance and emotion; (ii) a Perceptual-Cognitive reward that encourages [perception] and [think] processes that increase the likelihood of the reference response; (iii) answer accuracy to ensure faithfulness; and (iv) a dense format reward to enforce the desired structured output.
  Extensive experiments demonstrate that EBM-RL substantially outperforms text-only role-playing baselines and larger-scale vision-language models on our immersive role-playing benchmark, delivering simultaneous gains in visual-atmosphere consistency and character authenticity. Beyond the role-playing domain, EBM-RL also exhibits strong zero-shot generalization: without any additional fine-tuning, it consistently improves performance on out-of-domain VideoQA benchmarks. We additionally release an open-source dataset for video-grounded role-playing dialogue.

</details>


### [139] [AgentTrust: Runtime Safety Evaluation and Interception for AI Agent Tool Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04785)
*Chenglin Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentTrust 是一个运行时安全层，能在工具调用执行前拦截并返回结构化裁决（允许、警告、阻止、审查），结合反混淆归一化、安全修复建议、多步攻击链检测和 LLM 评判器，在低毫秒延迟下达到 95-96.7% 的裁决准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代 AI Agent 通过工具调用（文件操作、shell 命令、HTTP 请求、数据库查询）执行真实世界操作时，单个不安全行为（如意外删除、凭证泄露、数据窃取）可造成不可逆损害。现有防御方案不完整：事后基准测试无法事前阻止、静态防护无法应对混淆和多步上下文、基础设施沙箱只限制执行范围而不理解动作语义。

Method: AgentTrust 在工具调用执行前进行拦截，返回结构化裁决（allow/warn/block/review）。包含四个核心组件：shell 反混淆归一化器、SafeFix 安全替代建议、RiskChain 多步攻击链检测、以及缓存感知的 LLM-as-Judge 用于处理模糊输入。

Result: 在内部 300 场景基准上，生产规则集达到 95.0% 裁决准确率和 73.7% 风险级别准确率，端到端延迟为低毫秒级。在 630 个独立构建的真实世界对抗场景上（补丁规则集评估，非零样本），达到 96.7% 裁决准确率，包括 shell 混淆负载上约 93% 的准确率。

Conclusion: AgentTrust 作为运行时安全层，能有效检测和阻止 Agent 工具调用中的不安全行为，支持 AGPL-3.0 开源协议，并提供 Model Context Protocol（MCP）服务器以兼容 MCP Agent。

Abstract: Modern AI agents execute real-world side effects through tool calls such as file operations, shell commands, HTTP requests, and database queries. A single unsafe action, including accidental deletion, credential exposure, or data exfiltration, can cause irreversible harm. Existing defenses are incomplete: post-hoc benchmarks measure behavior after execution, static guardrails miss obfuscation and multi-step context, and infrastructure sandboxes constrain where code runs without understanding what an action means.
  We present AgentTrust, a runtime safety layer that intercepts agent tool calls before execution and returns a structured verdict: allow, warn, block, or review. AgentTrust combines a shell deobfuscation normalizer, SafeFix suggestions for safer alternatives, RiskChain detection for multi-step attack chains, and a cache-aware LLM-as-Judge for ambiguous inputs.
  We release a 300-scenario benchmark across six risk categories and an additional 630 independently constructed real-world adversarial scenarios. On the internal benchmark, the production-only ruleset achieves 95.0% verdict accuracy and 73.7% risk-level accuracy at low-millisecond end-to-end latency. On the 630-scenario benchmark, evaluated under a patched ruleset and not claimed as zero-shot, AgentTrust achieves 96.7% verdict accuracy, including about 93% on shell-obfuscated payloads. AgentTrust is released under the AGPL-3.0 license and provides a Model Context Protocol server for MCP-compatible agents.

</details>


### [140] [Strat-Reasoner: Reinforcing Strategic Reasoning of LLMs in Multi-Agent Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04906)
*Yidong He,Yutao Lai,Pengxu Yang,Jiarui Gan,Jiexin Wang,Yi Cai,Mengchen Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Strat-Reasoner框架，通过递归推理、集中式CoT比较和分组相对强化学习，提升LLM在多智能体博弈中的策略推理能力，平均性能提升22.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在多智能体博弈中表现不佳，因为其他智能体的非平稳性导致推理评估和信用分配困难，现有单/多智能体RL方法未将其他智能体纳入推理过程。

Method: 1) 递归推理范式：将其他智能体的推理过程整合到当前智能体的推理中；2) 集中式CoT比较模块：评估中间推理序列质量；3) 混合优势计算与分组相对RL优化策略。

Result: 在多种多智能体博弈任务上平均性能提升22.1%。

Conclusion: Strat-Reasoner有效提升了LLM在多智能体博弈中的策略推理能力，验证了递归推理和集中式CoT评估在复杂多智能体场景中的价值。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) excel in certain reasoning tasks, they struggle in multi-agent games where the final outcome depends on the joint strategies of all agents. In multi-agent games, the non-stationarity of other agents brings significant challenges on the evaluation of the reasoning process and the credit assignment over multiple reasoning steps. Existing single-agent reinforcement learning (RL) approaches and their multi-agent extensions fail to address these challenges as they do not incorporate other agents in the reasoning process. In this work, we propose Strat-Reasoner, a novel RL-based framework that improves LLMs' strategic reasoning ability in multi-agent games. We introduce a novel recursive reasoning paradigm where an agent's reasoning also integrates other agents' reasoning processes. To provide effective reward signals for the intermediate reasoning sequences, we employ a centralized Chain-of-Thought (CoT) comparison module to evaluate the reasoning quality. Finally, we compute an accurate hybrid advantage and develop a group-relative RL approach to optimize the LLM policy. Experimental results show that Strat-Reasoner substantially improves strategic abilities of underlying LLMs, achieving 22.1\% average performance improvements across various multi-agent games.

</details>


### [141] [A Foundation Model for Zero-Shot Logical Rule Induction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04916)
*Yin Jun Phua*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NRI是一种用于零样本规则归纳的预训练模型，通过统计特征表示文字而非具体谓词身份，结合并行槽位解码和可微规则执行，实现了无需重新训练即可跨任务迁移的符号推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有归纳逻辑编程方法是直推式的，其学习参数绑定于特定谓词，每遇到新任务都需要重新训练，缺乏泛化能力。

Method: 1) 使用统计编码器，将文字表示为与领域无关的统计特征（如类别条件概率、熵、共现率等）；2) 采用并行的槽位解码器，保持逻辑析取的置换不变性；3) 利用Product T-norm松弛使规则执行可微，实现端到端训练。

Result: 在规则恢复、对标签噪声和虚假鲁棒性、以及零样本迁移到真实世界基准任务上进行了评估。

Conclusion: 这项工作为符号推理的基础模型开辟了可能性。

Abstract: Inductive Logic Programming (ILP) learns interpretable logical rules from data. Existing methods are transductive: their learned parameters are bound to specific predicates and require retraining for each new task. We introduce Neural Rule Inducer (NRI), a pretrained model for zero-shot rule induction. Rather than encoding literal identities, NRI represents literals using domain-agnostic statistical properties such as class-conditional rates, entropy, and co-occurrence, which generalize across variable identities and counts without retraining. The model consists of a statistical encoder and a parallel slot-based decoder. Parallel decoding preserves the permutation invariance of logical disjunction; an autoregressive decoder would instead impose an arbitrary clause order. Product T-norm relaxation makes rule execution differentiable, allowing end-to-end training on prediction accuracy alone. We evaluate NRI on rule recovery, robustness to label noise and spurious correlations, and zero-shot transfer to real-world benchmarks, and we believe this work opens up the possibility of foundation models for symbolic reasoning. Code and the reference checkpoint are available at https://github.com/phuayj/neural-rule-inducer.

</details>


### [142] [On-line Learning in Tree MDPs by Treating Policies as Bandit Arms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04979)
*Anvay Shah,Ramsundar Anandanarayanan,Sharayu Moharir,Shivaram Kalyanakrishnan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出在树状马尔可夫决策问题（T-MDP）中，通过将每个策略视为一个臂，利用策略间共享数据的置信区间设计，使得经典Bandit算法（LUCB和UCB）能以多项式内存和计算量实现在线学习，并在样本复杂度和遗憾上取得优于现有方法的理论保证与实证表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: T-MDP（树状MDP）作为完美回忆序贯博弈中对抗固定对手的抽象模型，其在线学习问题（PAC和遗憾最小化）尚未被有效解决。直接对指数级策略应用Bandit算法面临计算爆炸问题，需要一种能共享数据、高效实现的方案。

Method: 将T-MDP中的每个策略建模为Bandit算法的一个臂；核心创新在于设计基于策略间共享数据的置信区间（confidence bounds），使得LUCB和UCB算法能够以多项式级别的内存和每步计算量实现；理论分析给出了依赖于每个终止状态（而非每个策略）的"间隙项"的样本复杂度与遗憾上界。

Result: 获得了实例依赖的样本复杂度和遗憾上界，其间隙项来自每个终止状态而非每个策略；在隐藏信息游戏套件上的实验表明，所提算法一致优于现有可选方法。

Conclusion: 通过巧妙地利用策略间共享数据设计置信区间，成功将经典Bandit算法高效应用于T-MDP，为树状结构序贯决策问题的在线学习提供了理论与实践俱优的解决方案。

Abstract: A Tree Markov Decision Problem (T-MDP) is a finite-horizon MDP with a starting state $s_{1}$, in which every state is reachable from $s_{1}$ through exactly one state-action trajectory. T-MDPs arise naturally as abstractions of decision making in sequential games with perfect recall, against stationary opponents. We consider the problem of on-line learning in T-MDPs, both in the PAC and the regret-minimisation regimes. We show that well-known bandit algorithms -- \textsc{Lucb} and \textsc{Ucb} -- can be applied on T-MDPs by treating each policy as an arm. The apparent technical challenge in this approach is that the number of policies is exponential in the number of states. Our main innovation is in the design of confidence bounds based on data shared by the policies, so that the bandit algorithms can yet be implemented with polynomial memory and per-step computation. We obtain instance-dependent upper bounds on sample complexity and regret that sum a ``gap term'' from every terminal state, rather than every policy. Empirically, our algorithms consistently outperform available alternatives on a suite of hidden-information games.

</details>


### [143] [Uno-Orchestra: Parsimonious Agent Routing via Selective Delegation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05007)
*Zhiqing Cui,Haotong Xie,Jiahao Yuan,Cheng Yang,Hanqing Wang,Yuxin Wu,Yifan Wu,Siru Zhong,Tao Yu,Yifu Guo,Siyu Zhang,Xinlei Yu,Qibing Ren,Usman Naseem*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Uno-Orchestra，一种统一编排策略，通过强化学习联合学习任务分解与子任务分配，在13个基准测试中达到77.0% macro pass@1，比最强基线高约16%，同时成本降低约一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体系统依赖刚性编排（扁平路由或手工任务分解），导致分解深度、工作节点选择和推理预算无法在一个统一目标下联合优化。

Method: Uno-Orchestra：一种统一编排策略，选择性分解任务并将每个子任务分配给可接受的（模型，原语）对，通过从真实交互轨迹中收集的RL轨迹联合学习两种决策。

Result: 在涵盖数学、代码、知识、长上下文和工具使用的13个基准测试中，与22个基线相比，Uno-Orchestra达到77.0% macro pass@1，比最强工作流基线高约16%，每查询成本低约一个数量级。

Conclusion: Uno-Orchestra推进了选择性委托的精度-效率边界，实现了准确性与成本之间的更优权衡。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) multi-agent systems typically rely on rigid orchestration, committing either to flat per-query routing or to hand-engineered task decomposition, so decomposition depth, worker choice, and inference budget are not jointly optimized under one objective. We introduce Uno-Orchestra, a unified orchestration policy that selectively decomposes a task and dispatches each subtask to an admissible (model, primitive) pair, with both decisions learned together from curated RL trajectories grounded in real worker interactions. Against 22 baselines on a 13-benchmark suite spanning math, code, knowledge, long-context, and agentic tool-use, Uno-Orchestra reaches 77.0% macro pass@1, roughly 16% above the strongest workflow baseline, at roughly an order of magnitude lower per-query cost, advancing the accuracy-efficiency frontier of selective delegation.

</details>


### [144] [Position: Embodied AI Requires a Privacy-Utility Trade-off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05017)
*Xiaoliang Fan,Jiarui Chen,Zhuodong Liu,Ziqi Yang,Peixuan Xu,Ruimin Shen,Junhui Liu,Jianzhong Qi,Cheng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出SPINE框架，主张将隐私视为整个具身AI生命周期的架构级约束，而非各阶段的独立特性，并通过多准则隐私分类矩阵实现跨阶段隐私控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前EAI系统在指令、感知、规划、交互等阶段的优化相互独立，未考虑高频部署中隐私泄露不可逆的问题，导致系统性隐私危机。

Method: 提出SPINE框架，将隐私作为动态控制信号贯穿EAI全生命周期，建立多准则隐私分类矩阵来协调各阶段之间的上下文敏感性。

Result: 通过初步仿真和真实案例验证了隐私约束在下游系统行为中的传播效应，表明碎片化的隐私补丁不足以应对问题。

Conclusion: 具身AI系统的隐私应当是生命周期级的架构约束而非局部特性，SPINE为未来安全且功能完整的EAI系统提供了研究方向。

Abstract: Embodied AI (EAI) systems are rapidly transitioning from simulations into real-world domestic and other sensitive environments. However, recent EAI solutions have largely demonstrated advancements within isolated stages such as instruction, perception, planning and interaction, without considering their coupled privacy implications in high-frequency deployments where privacy leakage is often irreversible. This position paper argues that optimizing these components independently creates a systemic privacy crisis when deployed in sensitive settings, thereby advancing the position that privacy in EAI is a life cycle-level architectural constraint rather than a stage-local feature. To address these challenges, we propose Secure Privacy Integration in Next-generation Embodied AI (SPINE), a unified privacy-aware framework that treats privacy as a dynamic control signal governing cross-stage coupling throughout the entire EAI life cycle. SPINE decomposes the EAI pipeline into various stages and establishes a multi-criterion privacy classification matrix to orchestrate contextual sensitivity across stage boundaries. We conduct preliminary simulation and real-world case studies to conceptually validate how privacy constraints propagate downstream to reshape system behavior, illustrating the insufficiency of fragmented privacy patches and motivating future research directions into secure yet functional embodied AI systems. We detail the SPINE framework and case studies at https://github.com/rminshen03/EAI_Privacy_Position.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用脚本化控制器、预定义世界模型接口、验证器程序和规划执行器，维护可执行Python世界模型，通过验证器验证观察，并基于MDL简约性偏好的简化抽象进行规划。

Abstract: We evaluate an initial coding-agent system for ARC-AGI-3 in which the agent maintains an executable Python world model, verifies it against previous observations, refactors it toward simpler abstractions as a practical proxy for an MDL-like simplicity bias, and plans through the model before acting. The system is intentionally direct: it uses a scripted controller, predefined world-model interfaces, verifier programs, and a plan executor, but no hand-coded game-specific logic. We report results on the 25 public ARC-AGI-3 games. Each recorded playthrough uses a fresh agent instance with no access to previous playthrough-specific files or conversation state. Most games have a single recorded playthrough; for a few games, we report multiple independent fresh-agent playthroughs to expose run-to-run variability. The agent fully solved 7 games, achieved a Relative Human Action Efficiency greater than 75%, on 6 games, and obtained a mean per-game RHAE of 32.58%. Because the system uses no game-specific code, it can serve as a game-general baseline for ARC-AGI-3. Performance on the private validation set remains to be tested. Overall, the results provide preliminary evidence that verifier-driven executable world models are a promising approach for ARC-AGI-3 agents.

### [146] [External Validation of Deep Learning Models for BI-RADS Breast Density Prediction from Ultrasound Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05082)
*Yuxuan Chen,Arianna Bunnell,Yanqi Xu,Haoyan Yang,Thomas K. Wolfgruber,John A. Shepherd,Yiqiu Shen*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本研究外部验证了三种深度学习模型（DenseNet121、ViT-B/32、ResNet50）从乳腺超声检查预测乳腺密度的能力，发现模型在极度致密型乳腺中表现最佳（AUROC 0.868-0.899），在异质性致密型乳腺中表现较低（0.699-0.729），且泛化性能良好。但在10年风险预测中，AI密度结合年龄的效果未显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证深度学习模型在外部独立队列中从乳腺超声预测乳腺密度的泛化能力，并评估AI衍生的乳腺密度在10年乳腺癌风险预测中的附加价值。

Method: 使用包含2,000例超声检查的外部验证集（500例癌症病例+1,500例对照），评估DenseNet121、ViT-B/32、ResNet50三种模型在四类乳腺密度（A/B/C/D）上的患者级AUROC；并将AI密度与年龄结合纳入Tyrer-Cuzick模型进行10年风险预测。

Result: 三种模型在极度致密型（D类）中表现最好（AUROC 0.868-0.899），在异质性致密型（C类）中表现最差（0.699-0.729）；DenseNet121整体最优（微平均AUROC 0.885）；AI密度+年龄的风险预测AUROC（0.541）低于传统方法（0.570），但差异不显著（p=0.23）。

Conclusion: 深度学习模型在乳腺密度评估中具有良好的外部泛化能力，但在异质性致密型乳腺上的表现仍是挑战；AI衍生的乳腺密度在10年风险预测中的增量价值有限，需进一步优化。

Abstract: We externally validated three deep learning models (DenseNet121, ViT-B/32, and ResNet50) for predicting mammographic breast density from breast ultrasound exams on an independent cohort. The external validation set comprised 2,000 ultrasound exams, including 500 cancer cases defined by an initial negative exam (BI-RADS 1 or 2) followed by a cancer diagnosis within 6 months to 10 years, and 1,500 negative controls matched by manufacturer and study year. Performance was measured using patient-level AUROC across four density categories: A (fatty), B (scattered), C (heterogeneous), and D (extremely dense). As a downstream assessment, we also evaluated 10-year risk prediction by incorporating age and AI-derived density into the Tyrer-Cuzick model and comparing performance against a reference model using age and mammography-reported density. All three models performed best in extremely dense breasts (AUROC 0.868-0.899), with strong performance in fatty (0.814-0.838) and scattered density (0.764-0.799), and lower performance in heterogeneously dense breasts (0.699-0.729). DenseNet121 achieved the highest overall performance (micro-averaged AUROC 0.885), and performance across categories was comparable between internal and external testing. For risk modeling, age combined with AI-derived density yielded a lower AUROC than age combined with mammography-reported density (0.541 vs. 0.570; p = 0.23), with no statistically significant difference. These findings indicate that deep learning models generalize well to external data with different racial composition for breast density assessment. While performance is strongest in extremely dense breasts, heterogeneously dense remains more challenging, highlighting the need for targeted optimization.

</details>


### [147] [CTseg: A Tool for Brain CT Segmentation, Spatial Normalisation, and Volumetrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05154)
*Mikael Brudfors*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: CTseg是一款免费的大脑CT图像分割、空间标准化和体积测量软件，基于Multi-Brain生成建模框架，可输出与SPM统一分割相同格式的组织图、变形场和脑体积估计。通过配对MR/CT扫描的系统验证，CTseg在分割精度、空间标准化一致性、脑体积一致性等方面显著优于直接将SPM的MRI分割方法应用于CT图像的基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CTseg虽已在临床研究中被采用（如中风、痴呆、脑形态测量等），但一直缺乏针对独立参考标准的系统验证。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过配对MR/CT头部扫描对CTseg进行全面验证。

Method: 使用配对MR/CT头部扫描数据，从四个维度评估CTseg：1) 分割精度（以MRI导出的银标准为参考）；2) 空间标准化一致性（组平均锐度和体素变异系数）；3) 脑体积一致性（组内相关系数和Bland-Altman分析）；4) 下游性别分类性能。基线方法为直接将SPM的MRI统一分割应用于CT图像。

Result: CTseg在分割和标准化方面显著优于基线方法，在全脑体积（TBV）一致性上表现更强，在颅内总体积（TIV）一致性上与基线相当。

Conclusion: CTseg是一种有效、可靠且可复现的脑CT分割和标准化工具，能够将SPM成熟的分析流程从MRI扩展到CT领域，且无需预处理或重采样即可应用于常规医院CT扫描。

Abstract: This paper presents and validates CTseg, a freely available software for brain CT segmentation, spatial normalisation, and volumetrics. CTseg builds on the Multi-Brain generative modelling framework, providing a CT-specific pipeline that produces tissue maps, deformation fields, and brain volume estimates in the same format as SPM's unified segmentation, thereby extending SPM's established analysis chain from MRI to CT. CTseg is designed for routine hospital CT scans without requiring preprocessing or resampling in deployment. Although CTseg has been adopted in clinical research spanning, among other things, stroke, dementia, and brain morphometry, a systematic validation against an independent reference standard has been lacking. Using paired MR/CT head scans, we evaluate CTseg across four dimensions: segmentation accuracy against an MRI-derived silver standard; spatial normalisation consistency through group-average sharpness and voxelwise coefficient of variation; brain volume agreement via intraclass correlation and Bland-Altman analysis; and downstream sex classification performance from normalised tissue maps. As a baseline, we apply SPM's MRI-based unified segmentation directly to the CT images. CTseg significantly outperformed this baseline for segmentation and normalisation, showed stronger TBV agreement, and achieved comparable TIV agreement. CTseg is freely available at https://github.com/WCHN/CTseg, and all experiment code is included in the repository for full reproducibility.

</details>


### [148] [MRI-Eval: A Tiered Benchmark for Evaluating LLM Performance on MRI Physics and GE Scanner Operations Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05175)
*Perry E. Radau*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出了MRI-Eval基准测试，用于评估LLM在MRI物理和GE扫描仪操作知识方面的能力。研究发现，模型在多选题上表现优异（93.2%-97.1%），但在去选项的自由回忆测试中性能大幅下降（最低13.8%），尤其GE扫描仪操作知识表现最差，表明高多选题分数掩盖了真实知识缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MRI LLM基准主要依赖教科书多选题，顶级模型已取得高分，缺乏区分度；且没有系统性评估研究型MRI实践中关键的厂商特定扫描仪操作知识。

Method: 构建了包含1365道题目的MRI-Eval基准，涵盖九个类别和三个难度层级，来源包括教科书、GE扫描仪手册、编程课程材料和专家生成问题。评估了五个模型家族，采用多选题（主要）、去选项+独立LLM评判（stem-only）和原始诊断条件三种测试方式。

Result: 多选题准确率93.2%-97.1%，GE扫描仪操作在所有模型中最低（88.2%-94.6%）。去选项测试中，前沿模型准确率降至58.4%-61.1%，Llama 3.3 70B降至37.1%；GE扫描仪操作去选项准确率仅为13.8%-29.8%。

Conclusion: 高多选题表现可能掩盖弱的自由文本回忆能力，特别是厂商特定操作知识。MRI-Eval更适合作为相对比较基准而非绝对能力度量，建议谨慎使用LLM原始输出进行GE特定协议指导。

Abstract: Background: Existing MRI LLM benchmarks rely mainly on review-book multiple-choice questions, where top proprietary models already score highly, limiting discrimination. No systematic benchmark has evaluated vendor-specific scanner operational knowledge central to research MRI practice. Purpose: We developed MRI-Eval, a tiered benchmark for relative model comparison on MRI physics and GE scanner operations knowledge using primary multiple-choice questions (MCQ), with stem-only and primed diagnostic conditions as complementary analyses. Methods: MRI-Eval includes 1365 scored items across nine categories and three difficulty tiers from textbooks, GE scanner manuals, programming course materials, and expert-generated questions. Five model families were evaluated (GPT-5.4, Claude Opus 4.6, Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 2.5 Pro, Llama 3.3 70B). MCQ was primary; stem-only removed options and used an independent LLM judge; primed stem-only tested responses to incorrect user claims. Results: Overall MCQ accuracy was 93.2% to 97.1%. GE scanner operations was the lowest category for every model (88.2% to 94.6%). In stem-only, frontier-model accuracy fell to 58.4% to 61.1%, and Llama 3.3 70B fell to 37.1%; GE scanner operations stem-only accuracy was 13.8% to 29.8%. Conclusion: High MCQ performance can mask weak free-text recall, especially for vendor-specific operational knowledge. MRI-Eval is most informative as a relative comparison benchmark rather than an absolute competency measure and supports caution in using raw LLM outputs for GE-specific protocol guidance.

</details>
